       <h2 class="text-center">
        Paperwritings.com: Paper Writing Service that Knows the Rules
       </h2>
       <p>
        Students are bombarded with tasks daily, but thankfully, Paper Writings is always there to help them out. If you are looking for an expert that will answer the call of the desperate student, then we are here to assist. With the deadline appearing closer, you are probably worried about homework becoming more complicated. After all, we have been on the market for quite some time to know that “write paper” request is not something that can be done overnight.
       </p>
       <p>
        Thankfully, our service has been rushing to alleviate the tension and offer some professional help. With various options included, such as dissertation writing, essays, reports, and more, we remain on top. Even if you think that a detailed assignment is not a motivation, we are willing to produce a 100% original composition. Hiring people with no experience may be easy, but we only strive to work with specialists who have a degree in the relevant discipline. This way, we as an online writing paper service assure you of the quality of the product.
       </p>
       <h2 class="text-center">
        Academic Experts for Help: Nail the College Homework
       </h2>
       <p>
        We are aware of the pressure that is being put on students. Are your days full of stress and you wish buying research paper would help? We have something more efficient than that: we are making a text to knock the teachers off their feet. First, we do in-depth research to determine the complexity of the paper. Secondly, we assign a specialist with the credentials to fit the task. Without any exaggeration on the part of the service, you’ll receive the task on the level that instantly puts it above the rest.
       </p>
       <p>
        It would be appropriate to mention the affordable prices at Paper Writings. It is no secret that many students instantly regret their decisions to use customer service because of the fees. We are not thrilled about the prospect of leaving the learners on a shoestring budget. This is the reason we are so concerned about the privacy policy and the concept of free revision by a paper writer. Be ready to improve the grades with our assistance.  If you are seeking assistance for the first time, we have a support team to provide you with answers.

  <script>
   $(document).ready(function () {
                                    function setCookie(cname, cvalue, exdays) {
                                        var d = new Date();
                                        d.setTime(d.getTime() + (exdays * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
                                        var expires = "expires=" + d.toUTCString();
                                        document.cookie = cname + "=" + cvalue + ";" + expires + ";path=/";
                                    }
                                    function getCookie(cname) {
                                        var name = cname + "=";
                                        var decodedCookie = decodeURIComponent(document.cookie);
                                        var ca = decodedCookie.split(';');
                                        for (var i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
                                            var c = ca[i];
                                            while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') {
                                                c = c.substring(1);
                                            }
                                            if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) {
                                                return c.substring(name.length, c.length);
                                            }
                                        }
                                        return "";
                                    }
                                    if (getCookie('cookie-banner') !== 'show-banner') {
                                        $("#cookie-banner").fadeIn(1000).addClass('cookie-banner-show');
                                    }
                                    $("#hide-cookie-banner").on('click', function () {
                                        setCookie('cookie-banner', 'show-banner');
                                        $("#cookie-banner").fadeOut(1000).removeClass('cookie-banner-show');
                                    });


                                    if (getCookie('pay_later-banner') !== 'show-banner') {
                                        $("#pay_later-banner").fadeIn(1000);
                                    }
                                    $("#close-pay_later-banner").on('click', function () {
                                        setCookie('pay_later-banner', 'show-banner');
                                        $("#pay_later-banner").fadeOut(1000);
                                    });


                                    $("#owl-testimonials").owlCarousel({
                                        navigation: true,
                                        slideSpeed: 300,
                                        paginationSpeed: 400,
                                        singleItem: true,
                                        autoPlay: false,
                                        navigation : true,
                                                autoHeight: true,
                                        navigationText: ["<i class='fa fa-angle-left'></i>", "<i class='fa fa-angle-right'></i>"],
                                        itemsCustom: [
                                            [0, 1],
                                            [450, 1],
                                            [600, 1],
                                            [700, 2],
                                            [1000, 2],
                                            [1200, 2],
                                            [1400, 2],
                                            [1600, 2]
                                        ]
                                    });

                                });
